<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rumoer.html>rumoer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ish, -y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rumoerig.html>rumoerig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rumoerig.html>rumoeriger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">rumoerigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>noisy, loud</li>
<li>boisterous, audibly restless, tumultuous to riotous</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rund.html>rund</a> (10105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:runt.html>runt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:rund.html>rund</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrunþaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rund.html>rund</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:runderen.html>runderen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rundje.html>rundje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>any bovine animal</li>
<li>idiot, stupid person

***rups.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rups.html>rups</a> (22117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rupse</i>, from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rupsene</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūpō</i> and probably related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raupijaną</i>. 
</p><p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Raupe</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">rûp</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rups.html>rups</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rupsen.html>rupsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rupsje.html>rupsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A caterpillar, the <a href = vnd.unilang:larve.html>larve</a> of a butterfly.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rus.html>rus</a> (8222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rusch</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rosch</i>. The <span class="Latn" lang="la">Juncaceae</span> plants may constitute a parallel etymology
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rus.html>rus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:russen.html>russen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rus.html>rusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sod.html>sod</a></span>, turf of <span class="Latn" lang="en">soil</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">grass</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:reed.html>reed</a></span> or other vegetation</li>
<li>The graminal plant <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Armeria_vulgaris" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Armeria vulgaris"><i>Armeria <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i></a></span> or <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Armeria_maritima" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Armeria maritima"><i>Armeria maritima</i></a></span></li>
<li>A grass-like plant, (<a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a>)<span class="Latn" lang="en">rush</span>, notably of the genera <i>Juncus</i> and <i>Luzula</i>.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:sod.html>sod</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">plag</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zode.html>zode</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i>Armeria</i> species</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">pastoorsgras</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plant rush</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bies.html>bies</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bloembies</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">veldbies</span></li></ul>

***rusk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rusk.html>rusk</a> (44726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span></span> or <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">rosca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a twist or roll of bread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusk.html>rusk</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">rusks</b>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Zwieback_auf_Holzbrett.jpg/220px-Zwieback_auf_Holzbrett.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Zwieback_auf_Holzbrett.jpg/330px-Zwieback_auf_Holzbrett.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Zwieback_auf_Holzbrett.jpg/440px-Zwieback_auf_Holzbrett.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="600" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i>Zwieback</i></div></div></div>
<ol><li>a rectangular, hard, dry biscuit
<ul><li><b>1719:</b> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daniel_Defoe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Daniel Defoe"><a href = vnd.unilang:daniel.html>Daniel</a> Defoe</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robinson_Crusoe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robinson Crusoe">Robinson Crusoe</a></i>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> he <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> a large basket of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rusk.html>rusk</a></b> or biscuit, and three jars of fresh water, into the boat.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>a twice-baked bread, <a href = vnd.unilang:slices.html>slices</a> of bread baked until they are hard and crisp (also called a <i>zwieback</i>)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1956</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Delano_Ames" class="extiw" title="w:Delano Ames"><a href = vnd.unilang:delano.html>Delano</a> Ames</a>,  chapter 25, in  <cite>Crime out of Mind</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5915292W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A newly-arrived couple at the next table <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> admitted that “this <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> more like” and that if the Alpenrose could also produce a proper cup of tea it would be just like home. Bill Andreyef, who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> eating a lightly-boiled egg and a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rusk.html>rusk</a></b>, regarded the other <a href = vnd.unilang:diners.html>diners</a> with resentment.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>a weaning food for children</li>
<li>a cereal binder used in meat product manufacture</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Brussels biscuit</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">twice-baked bread</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">zwieback</span></li></ul>
</body> 
***russ.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:russ.html>russ</a> (7460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrussą</i>, (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">hross</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">horse</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:hors.html>hors</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">hoars</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ros.html>ros</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ross</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱr̥sos</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">car</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wagon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">currus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chariot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱers-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hurry</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gmq-osw"><a href = vnd.unilang:russ.html>russ</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>a horse <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">equine mammal</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still somewhat used in two dialects, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gotlandic" class="extiw" title="w:Gotlandic">Gotlandic</a> and the dialect of Bohuslän.</li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a> (993)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruste.html>ruste</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rusta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rustijō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusten.html>rusten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a>, calm, peace
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:waarom.html>Waarom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a></b>?</i></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Why don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> you leave <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b>alone</b>?</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">Why don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> you leave <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> at <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a></b>?</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> half-time</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a></strong>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rustiek.html>rustiek</a> (53334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rustiek.html>rustiek</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rustiek.html>rustieker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">rustiekst</b>)

<ol><li>rustic</li>
<li>unrefined, uneducated, uncivilised</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***rusty.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a> (8359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">rustiġ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rustagaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">rusterch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">rustich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">roastich</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roestig.html>roestig</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">rusterig</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">rüsterig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">rostig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">rostig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">rustier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">rustiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Marked or corroded by <a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a>. <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span></li>
<li>Of the <a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a> color, reddish or reddish-brown. <span class="defdate">[from 14th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1855</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Browning" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Browning">Robert Browning</a>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Childe_Roland_to_the_Dark_Tower_Came" class="extiw" title="s:Childe Roland to the Dark Tower Came">“Childe Roland to the Dark Tower Came”</a>, XIV:
<dl><dd>Alive? he might be dead for aught I know, / With that red <a href = vnd.unilang:gaunt.html>gaunt</a> and colloped neck a-strain, / And shut <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> underneath the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:manen.html>mane</a>;</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1914</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Louis_Joseph_Vance" class="extiw" title="w:Louis Joseph Vance"><a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Joseph Vance</a>,  chapter I, in  <cite>Nobody</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_H._Doran_Company" class="extiw" title="w:George H. Doran Company">George H[enry] Doran Company</a>, published 1915, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/40817384">40817384</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>Three chairs of the steamer type, all maimed, comprised the furniture of this roof-garden, with<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>on one of the copings a row of four red <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> flower-pots filled with sun-baked dust from which gnarled and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></b> stalks thrust themselves up like withered elfin limbs.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Lacking recent experience, out of practice, especially with respect to a skill or activity. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b> December 29,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a> Sheringham,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport1/hi/football/eng_prem/9308904.stm">Liverpool 0-1 Wolverhampton</a>”, in  <cite>BBC</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Before the match, Hodgson <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> expressed the hope that his players would be fresh rather than <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></b> after an 18-day break from league commitments because of two successive postponements.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now chiefly historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of clothing, especially dark clothing: worn, shabby. <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1911</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Max_Beerbohm" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Max Beerbohm"><a href = vnd.unilang:max.html>Max</a> Beerbohm</a>, <i>Zuleika Dobson</i>:
<dl><dd>He wore a black jacket, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></b> and amorphous.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Affected with the fungal plant disease called <a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Variant form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">resty</i>; compare also <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">reasty</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Discolored and rancid; reasty. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:rusty.html>rusty</a></b> bacon</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ruw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruw.html>ruw</a> (5589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ruuch</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ru.html>ru</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rou</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rūh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rū</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rūhwaz</i>. The original <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> ended in <i>-h-</i>, which disappeared between vowels, giving <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rū-</i> in the inflected forms in Old Dutch. This then <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> rise to an alternative uninflected form <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rū</i>, which developed into Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ru.html>ru</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rou</i>, modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruw.html>ruw</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rouw.html>rouw</a></i>. The original uninflected form <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> back-formed to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruig.html>ruig</a></i> based on other <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> with <i>-ch</i> in the uninflected form and <i>-g-</i> in inflected forms, similar to what happened to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruw.html>ruw</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruwer.html>ruwer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ruwst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rough, crude, harsh <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">not gentle</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>raw, crude <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">unprocessed</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ruwe.html>ruwe</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:suiker.html>suiker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:binnenbrengen.html>binnengebracht</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>raw</b> sugar enters the building right here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijproduct.html>bijproduct</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ruwe.html>ruwe</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:olie.html>olie</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a byproduct of <b>crude</b> oil.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***ryge.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ryge.html>ryge</a> (88559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*rugi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rugiz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wrugʰyo-</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рожь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rožʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">rugis</i>).
</p><p>See also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">rogga</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:rogge.html>rogge</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">roggo</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Rogg</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rogge.html>rogge</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:rocko.html>rocko</a></i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:roggen.html>Roggen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:rocken.html>Rocken</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">rugr</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = lang="sv">råg</i>).

***sabbelen.html

<p>Variant of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">zabberen</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">zabben</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i>. The change from initial <i>z</i> to <i>s</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> irregular.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sabot.html>sabot</a> (88551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:sabot.html>sabot</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ciabatta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sabot.html>sabot</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sabots</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A wooden shoe.
<ul><li><b>1974</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GB_Edwards" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:GB Edwards">GB Edwards</a>, <i>The Book of Ebenezer Le Page</i>, New York 2007, p. 8:
<dl><dd>She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a tiny little woman and wore big <b>sabots</b> and a big scoop.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A carrier around projectile(s) in firearms, cannons and artillery which holds the projectile in precision within the barrel</li></ol>
</body>

***sadist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sadist.html>sadist</a> (18925)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the name of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marquis_de_Sade" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Marquis de Sade">Marquis <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sade.html>Sade</a></a>; see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sadism</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sadist.html>sadist</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sadists</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who derives pleasure through cruelty or pain to others.</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:sadist.html>sadist</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
